<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nachtrust.html>nachtrust</a> (15787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nachtruste</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nacht.html>nacht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a></i>.

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:night.html>night</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>, nightly <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:sleep.html>sleep</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a> (20042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaren</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:fall.html>fall</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:autumn.html>autumn</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:season.html>season</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:summer.html>summer</a>)
<ul><li><b>1698</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Blankaart, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:den.html>Den</a> Neder-landschen herbarius <a href = vnd.unilang:ofte.html>ofte</a> kruid-boek <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamste.html>voornaamste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruiden.html>kruiden</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jan.html>Jan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ten.html>ten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://dbnl.nl/tekst/blan012nede01_01/blan012nede01_01_0379.php">463</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewas.html>gewas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dry.html>dry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voeten.html>voeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:water.html>water</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikke.html>dikke</a>, geknoopte <a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stam.html>stam</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sig.html>sig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verscheiden.html>verscheide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:takken.html>takken</a> verdeelende, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a></b> geelagtig <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> crop grows <a href = vnd.unilang:up.html>up</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:three.html>three</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>high</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:above.html>above</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:water.html>water</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thick.html>thick</a>, noded <a href = vnd.unilang:green.html>green</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>, branching <a href = vnd.unilang:into.html>into</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:several.html>several</a> twigs, <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> yellows <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fall.html>fall</a></b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nakie.html>nakie</a> (27026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:naked.html>naked</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:nude.html>nude</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">colloquial Hollandic <a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nakie.html>nakie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nakie.html>nakies</a></b>)
